namespace = darkages

character_event = { 		#Event that calls the spouse through event to add a courtier as friend as a single day must pass for the interface to update
	id = darkages.72469		#This hidden event sets everything in motion
	title = EVTNAME1972469
	desc = EVTDESC1972469
	picture = GFX_evt_da_private_discussion
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	hide_window = yes
	
	trigger = {
		is_married = yes
		is_landed = yes
		
		NOT = { 
			has_character_modifier = da_framed_courtier_tmp 
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1200
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			spouse = { trait = just }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			spouse = { trait = honest }	
		}
		
	}
	
	immediate = {
		random_courtier_or_vassal = {
			limit = {
				ai = yes
				is_adult = yes
				NOT = { spouse = { character = ROOT } }
			}
			
			save_event_target_as = darkages_framed_courtier
			
	
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = da_framed
				duration = 1763			
			}
			
		}
		
		spouse = {
			save_event_target_as = darkages_framed_courtier_spouse
			character_event = { id = darkages.72470 days = 7 }
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = da_framed_courtier_tmp
			duration = 3650
			hidden = yes
		}
		
	}
	
	
}


character_event = { 		#Event that assigns the selected courtier as a new friend in order to allow the text to make sense
	id = darkages.72470
	title = EVTNAME1972470
	desc = EVTDESC1972470
	picture = GFX_evt_da_private_discussion
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {

	}
	

	immediate = {
	
		add_friend = event_target:darkages_framed_courtier	
	
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = darkages.72471 days = 7 }	#Calls the player and the story starts
		}		
		
	}
	

}

character_event = { 		#Called by on_death action - if spouse of dieing character has Manipulative Spouse modifier remove it
	id = darkages.72508
	title = EVTNAME1972508
	desc = EVTDESC1972508
	picture = GFX_evt_da_private_discussion
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_religion
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		spouse = { has_character_modifier = da_spouse_manipulator }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		spouse = { character_event = { id = darkages.72509 } }
	}

	
}

character_event = { 		#affected spouse is not under the influence of the dieing character

	trigger = {

	}
	
	immediate = {
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA1972509
		
		remove_character_modifier = da_spouse_manipulator
		
	}	

	
}

character_event = { 		#Setup event
	id = darkages.72513
	title = EVTNAME1972513
	desc = EVTDESC1972513
	picture = GFX_evt_da_carriage
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_diplomacy
	
	trigger = {
		is_landed = yes
		is_married = yes		

		NOT = { 
			has_character_modifier = da_travelling_spouse_tmp 
		}

		spouse = {
			NOR = { 
				trait = pregnant
				has_disease_trigger = yes
				has_symptom_trigger = yes
				has_minor_disease_trigger = yes
				is_incapable = yes
				trait = resting
				has_injury_trigger = yes
				age = 60
			}
		}

	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1200
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			spouse = { trait = ambitious }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			spouse = { trait = gregarious }	
		}		
		
	}


	
	immediate = {
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = da_travelling_spouse_tmp

########################################################################
#
#	CONTROL EVENT THAT APPLIES/REMOVES THE LACK OF HARMONY MODIFIERS
#
########################################################################

#####################################################################################################

character_event = { 		#Checks if character is entitled to a lack of harmony modifier and applies it
	id = darkages.72515
	title = EVTNAME1972515
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC1972515_1
		trigger = {
			spouse = {
				NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT	value = 0 } }
				opinion = { who = ROOT	value = -10 }
			}			
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC1972515_2
		trigger = {
			spouse = {
				NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT	value = -10 } }
				opinion = { who = ROOT	value = -25 }
			}			
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = EVTDESC1972515_3
		trigger = {
			spouse = {
				NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT	value = -25 } }
			}			
		}
	}	
	picture = GFX_evt_da_bad_news
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	trigger = {
		is_landed = yes
		
		spouse = {
			NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT	value = 0 } }
		}
		
		NOR = {
			trait = patient
			spouse = { trait = patient }
		}
		
		NOR = {
			AND = {
				spouse = {
					NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT	value = 0 } }
					opinion = { who = ROOT	value = -10 }
				}
				has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_1
			}
			
			AND = {
				spouse = {
					NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT	value = -10 } }
					opinion = { who = ROOT	value = -25 }
				}
				has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_2
			}

			AND = {
				spouse = {
					NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT	value = -25 } }
				}
				has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_3
			}			
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 120
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = wroth
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			spouse = { trait = wroth }
		}
		
	}
	
	immediate = {
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA1972515
		trigger = {
			spouse = {
				NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT	value = 0 } }
				opinion = { who = ROOT	value = -10 }
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = DA_CUSTOMTOOLTIP220 }
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_3
			}
				
			remove_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_3
		}
			
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_2
			}
			
			remove_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_2
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = da_lack_harmony_1
			duration = 1825
		}
			
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB1972515
		trigger = {
			spouse = {
				NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT	value = -10 } }
				opinion = { who = ROOT	value = -25 }
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = DA_CUSTOMTOOLTIP220 }
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_3
			}
				
			remove_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_3
		}
			
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_1
			}
			
			remove_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_1
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = da_lack_harmony_2
			duration = 1825
		}
			
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTC1972515
		trigger = {
			spouse = {
				NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT	value = -25 } }
			}		
		}
		custom_tooltip = { text = DA_CUSTOMTOOLTIP220 }
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_2
			}
				
			remove_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_2
		}
			
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_1
			}
			
			remove_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_1
		}

		add_character_modifier = {
			name = da_lack_harmony_3
			duration = 1825
		}
			
		
	}	
	
}

		}

		}

	desc = EVTDESC1972517
	picture = GFX_evt_da_easter

character_event = { 		#Called from 72524, depicting what happened after the player decided to counter the spouse's decision
	id = darkages.72521
	title = EVTNAME1972521
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = da_argument_w
		}
		text = EVTDESC1972521_1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = da_argument_l
		}
		text = EVTDESC1972521_2
	}	
	picture = GFX_evt_da_gold_chest
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_economy

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	
	}
	
	
	immediate = {

	}

	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA1972521
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = da_argument_w
		}

		prestige = 35

		event_target:da_travel_spouse = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = da_opinion_disgusted
				years = 5
			}
			
			remove_trait = travelling
			
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = da_wanderlust
				duration = -1
				stacking = yes
			}			
			
			
		}

		
		clr_character_flag =  da_opt1
		clr_character_flag =  da_opt2
		clr_character_flag =  da_opt3
		clr_character_flag =  da_opt4	

		clr_character_flag = da_argument_w			
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB1972521
		trigger = {
			has_character_flag = da_argument_l
		}

				
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag =  da_opt1 }
			treasury = -50
			prestige = -30
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag =  da_opt2 }
			treasury = -100
			prestige = -60			
		}		
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag =  da_opt3 }
			treasury = -150
			prestige = -90			
		}		
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_flag =  da_opt4 }
			treasury = -200
			prestige = -120
		}		
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_character_modifier = da_political_victory }
			remove_character_modifier = da_political_victory
		}
		
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = da_politically_beaten
			duration = 1825
		}

		event_target:da_travel_spouse = {
			prestige = 75
			
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = da_wanderlust
				duration = -1
				stacking = yes
			}			
			
		}		
		
		clr_character_flag =  da_opt1
		clr_character_flag =  da_opt2
		clr_character_flag =  da_opt3
		clr_character_flag =  da_opt4	

		clr_character_flag = da_argument_l		
		
	}	
	
}

character_event = { 		#Spouse defects to host realm and starts a love relationship with him/her
	id = darkages.72527
	title = EVTNAME1972527
	desc = EVTDESC1972527
	picture = GFX_evt_da_bad_news
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	

	}
	
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						event_target:da_travel_spouse = { is_female = no }
						event_target:event_target:da_travel_visited = { is_female = no }
					}
					AND = {
						event_target:da_travel_spouse = { is_female = yes }
						event_target:event_target:da_travel_visited = { is_female = yes }
					}					
				}
			}
			
			event_target:da_travel_visited = { add_trait = homosexual }
			event_target:da_travel_spouse = { add_trait = homosexual }			
			
		}

	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA1972527
		custom_tooltip = { text = DA_CUSTOMTOOLTIP244 }	
		
		prestige = -200
		
		event_target:da_travel_spouse = {
			remove_spouse = ROOT
			move_character = event_target:da_travel_visited	

			remove_trait = travelling
			
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = da_wanderlust
				duration = -1
				stacking = yes
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:da_travel_visited = { can_marry = yes }
					OR = {
						AND = {
							event_target:da_travel_spouse = { is_female = no }
							event_target:event_target:da_travel_visited = { is_female = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							event_target:da_travel_spouse = { is_female = yes }
							event_target:event_target:da_travel_visited = { is_female = no }
						}					
					}					
					
				}
				
				religion = event_target:da_travel_visited
				add_spouse = event_target:da_travel_visited
				add_lover = event_target:da_travel_visited				
				
			}
			else = {
				add_lover = event_target:da_travel_visited
			}
			
		}		
		
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTB1972527
		trigger = {
			NOR = {
				trait = kind
				trait = just
			}
		}		
		custom_tooltip = { text = DA_CUSTOMTOOLTIP243 }	
		
		prestige = -100
		
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = wroth } }

			random = {
				chance = 60
				add_trait = wroth
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { trait = cruel } }

			random = {
				chance = 60
				add_trait = cruel
			}
		}		
		
		event_target:da_travel_spouse = {
			remove_spouse = ROOT
			move_character = event_target:da_travel_visited	

			remove_trait = travelling
			
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = da_wanderlust
				duration = -1
				stacking = yes
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:da_travel_visited = { can_marry = yes }
					OR = {
						AND = {
							event_target:da_travel_spouse = { is_female = no }
							event_target:event_target:da_travel_visited = { is_female = yes }
						}
						AND = {
							event_target:da_travel_spouse = { is_female = yes }
							event_target:event_target:da_travel_visited = { is_female = no }
						}					
					}					
					
				}
				
				religion = event_target:da_travel_visited
				add_spouse = event_target:da_travel_visited
				add_lover = event_target:da_travel_visited				
				
			}
			else = {
				add_lover = event_target:da_travel_visited
			}
			
		}		
		
	}
	
}

	}

	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA1972530
		custom_tooltip = { text = DA_CUSTOMTOOLTIP249 }
		
		prestige = -200
		
		event_target:da_travel_spouse = {
			
			remove_trait = travelling
			
			random = {
				chance = 30
				add_trait = severely_injured
			}
			
			prestige = 50
			
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = da_wanderlust
				duration = -1
				stacking = yes
			}
			
		}		
		
		any_playable_ruler = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					religion = ROOT
					culture = ROOT
				}
			}
		
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = da_opinion_d_diplomacy
				years = 6
			}
		
		}
		
	}
	
}

		}

	}

	id = darkages.72538
	title = EVTNAME1972538
	desc = EVTDESC1972538
	picture = GFX_evt_da_private_discussion
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	trigger = {
	
		has_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_ruler
	
		spouse = {
			NOR = {
				has_job_title = job_chancellor
				has_job_title = job_marshal
				has_job_title = job_treasurer
				has_job_title = job_spymaster			
			}
				
			is_incapable = no
			NOT = { trait = resting }
			prisoner = no
			
			OR = {
				has_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_d
				has_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_m
				has_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_s
				has_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_e			
			}
			
		}

	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}
	
	immediate = {
	
		spouse = {
			remove_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_d
			remove_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_m
			remove_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_s
			remove_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_e
		}
		
		remove_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_ruler
		

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_3
			}
				
			remove_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_3
		}
			
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_2
			}
				
			remove_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_2
		}		
			
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_1
			}
			
			remove_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_1
		}		
		
		
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA1972538
		
		add_character_modifier = {
			name = da_lack_harmony_3
			duration = 1825
		}		
		
		spouse = {
		
			
			hidden_tooltip = {
			
				remove_opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_given_council_position_2 
				}		
			}
		
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = da_opinion_incensed
				years = 15
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					is_lover = ROOT
				}
				
				random = {
					chance = 75
					remove_lover = ROOT
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 } }
				}
				
				random = {
					chance = 40
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						trait = cruel
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.25
						trait = envious
					}				
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						trait = wroth
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.5
						trait = kind
					}				
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.75
						trait = temperate
					}					
					modifier = {
						factor = 0.66
						trait = patient
					}					
					
					add_rival = ROOT
				}
			}			


		}
		
	}

	id = darkages.72539
	title = EVTNAME1972539
	desc = EVTDESC1972539
	picture = GFX_evt_da_private_discussion
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	hide_window = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	
		OR = {
		
			AND = {
				has_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_ruler
	
				AND = {
					spouse = {
						OR = {
							has_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_d
							has_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_m
							has_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_s
							has_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_e			
						}
						
					}
				}
			}
			
			AND = {
				spouse = { has_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_ruler }
	
				OR = {
					has_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_d
					has_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_m
					has_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_s
					has_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_e			
				}
					
			}			
			
			
		}

	}
	
	immediate = {
	
		spouse = {
			remove_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_d
			remove_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_m
			remove_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_s
			remove_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_e
			remove_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_ruler			
		}
		
		remove_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_ruler
		remove_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_d
		remove_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_m
		remove_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_s
		remove_character_modifier = da_spouse_promised_council_e		
		
		
	}
	
}

			}

			da_lack_harmony_3 = {
				remove_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_3
				
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = da_lack_harmony_2
					duration = 720
				}
			}			
		}
		
		event_target:darkages_heir_spouse = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					add_friend = ROOT
				}
				2 = {
					add_lover = ROOT
				}
				17 = {
					custom_tooltip = { text = DA_CUSTOMTOOLTIP273 }
				}
			}
		
		}

	}
	
}


character_event = {		#Player & spouse keep their positions respectively. Player able to set education. Heir might take advantage of situation and decide for himself
	id = darkages.72559
	title = EVTNAME1972559
	desc = EVTDESC1972559
	picture = GFX_evt_da_couple_quarrel
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_war

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		
	}
	
	immediate = {
	
		remove_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_1
		remove_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_2
		remove_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_3	
	
		clr_character_flag = da_education_learning
		clr_character_flag = da_education_diplomacy
		clr_character_flag = da_education_martial
		clr_character_flag = da_education_stewardship
		clr_character_flag = da_education_intrigue
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA1972559
		custom_tooltip = { text = DA_CUSTOMTOOLTIP274 }
		
		prestige = -10
		piety = -20
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_1
					has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_2
					has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_3					
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				5 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						event_target:darkages_heir_spouse = { trait = kind }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						event_target:darkages_heir_spouse = { trait = patient }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						event_target:darkages_heir_spouse = { trait = cheerful }
					}

					add_character_modifier = {
						name = da_lack_harmony_1
						duration = 1460
					}
					
				}
				4 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						event_target:darkages_heir_spouse = { trait = cynical }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						event_target:darkages_heir_spouse = { trait = just }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						event_target:darkages_heir_spouse = { trait = dour }
					}

					add_character_modifier = {
						name = da_lack_harmony_2
						duration = 1460
					}				
				}
				3 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 2
						event_target:darkages_heir_spouse = { trait = wroth }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.75
						event_target:darkages_heir_spouse = { trait = cruel }
					}
					modifier = {
						factor = 1.5
						event_target:darkages_heir_spouse = { trait = envious }
					}

					add_character_modifier = {
						name = da_lack_harmony_3
						duration = 1460
					}				
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_1
				}
				
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = da_lack_harmony_2
					duration = 1825
				}
					
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_2
						has_character_modifier = da_lack_harmony_3
					}
				}
				
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = da_lack_harmony_3
					duration = 1825
				}
					
			}			
		
		}
		
		event_target:darkages_heir_spouse = {	
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = da_opinion_incensed
				years = 15
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random = {
				chance = 15
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					event_target:darkages_heir_heir = {	
						OR = {
							trait = willful
							trait = rowdy
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					event_target:darkages_heir_heir = {	
						OR = {
							trait = brooding
							trait = haughty
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 2
					event_target:darkages_heir_heir = {	
						OR = {
							trait = cruel
							trait = wroth
							trait = envious
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					event_target:darkages_heir_heir = {	
						OR = {
							trait = affectionate
							trait = conscientious 
						}
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.5
					event_target:darkages_heir_heir = {	
						OR = {
							trait = kind
							trait = patient
							trait = temperate
						}
					}
				}				
				character_event = { id = darkages.72561 }
			}
		}
		

	}
	
}
